11/22/22, 13:13 - Likith Dsi: import java.util.*;
public class Student 
{
  String usn,name,branch;
  long phone;
   Student(String u,String name,String br,long ph){
        this.usn = u;
        this.name = name;
        this.branch=br;
        this.phone=ph;
    }
   
  void displayStudent()
  {
    System.out.println("**********************");
    System.out.println("USN ="+usn);
    System.out.println("NAME ="+name);
    System.out.println("BRANCH ="+branch);
    System.out.println("PHONE NUMBER ="+phone);
    System.out.println("**********************");
  }
  public static void main(String args[])
  {
    Student st[]=new Student[100];
    Scanner ip=new Scanner(System.in);
    
    System.out.println("Enter the number of students");
    int n=ip.nextInt();
    //for(int i=0;i<n;i++)
       // st[i]=new Student();
    for(int j=0;j<n;j++)
    {
        System.out.println("Enter the USN,Name,Branch,Phone Number");
        String u=ip.next();
        String name=ip.next();
        String br=ip.next();
        long ph=ip.nextLong();
        st[j]=new Student(u,name,br,ph);
    }
    for(int m=0;m<n;m++)
    {
        System.out.format("Student %d details are\n",m+1);
        st[m].displayStudent();
    }
  }
}

1/6/23, 09:52 - Mohin Dsatm: // C++ program to demonstrate the working of friend function

#include <iostream>
using namespace std;

class Distance {
    private:
        int meter;
        
        // friend function
        friend int addFive(Distance);

    public:
        Distance() : meter(0) {}
        
};

// friend function definition
int addFive(Distance d) {

    //accessing private members from the friend function
    d.meter += 5;
    return d.meter;
}

int main() {
    Distance D;
    cout << "Distance: " << addFive(D);
    return 0;
}

3/7/23, 12:40 - Koustav Biswas DSATM: package swing2;

import javax.swing.*;
import java.awt.*;
import java.awt.event.*;

public class Calculator extends JFrame implements ActionListener {

	private JTextField display;

    // Constructor
    public Calculator() {
        super(" Calculator");

        // Set up display
        display = new JTextField();
        display.setEditable(false);
        display.setHorizontalAlignment(JTextField.RIGHT);

        // Set up buttons
        //command is button we have pressed
        //gettext which is present here and set text will update the get text
        String[][] buttonLabels = {
                {"7", "8", "9", "/"},
                {"4", "5", "6", "*"},
                {"1", "2", "3", "-"},
                {"0", ".", "=", "+"},
                {"clr"}
        };
        JPanel buttonPanel = new JPanel(new GridLayout(5, 5, 5, 5));
        for (int row = 0; row < 4; row++) 
        {
            for (int col = 0; col < 4; col++) 
            {
                JButton button = new JButton(buttonLabels[row][col]);
                button.addActionListener(this);
                buttonPanel.add(button);
            }
        }
        JButton button = new JButton(buttonLabels[4][0]);
        button.addActionListener(this);
        buttonPanel.add(button);

        // Set up layout
        setLayout(new BorderLayout());
        add(display, BorderLayout.NORTH);
        add(buttonPanel, BorderLayout.CENTER);

        // Set up window
        setDefaultCloseOperation(JFrame.EXIT_ON_CLOSE);
        setSize(300, 300);
        setVisible(true);
    }

    // Handle button clicks
    public void actionPerformed(ActionEvent event) {
        String command = event.getActionCommand();
        if ("0123456789.".contains(command)) {
            display.setText(display.getText() + command);
            
            
        } else if ("clr".contains(command)) {
            display.setText("");}
        else if ("+-*/".contains(command)) {
            display.setText(display.getText() + " " + command + " ");
        } else if ("=".equals(command)) {
            String[] tokens = display.getText().split(" ");//split space will go to next element when it gets a space 
            double result = Double.parseDouble(tokens[0]);
            for (int i = 1; i < tokens.length; i += 2) {
                String operator = tokens[i];
                double operand = Double.parseDouble(tokens[i+1]);
                if ("+".equals(operator)) {
                    result += operand;
                } else if ("-".equals(operator)) {
                    result -= operand;
                } else if ("*".equals(operator)) {
                    result *= operand;
                } else if ("/".equals(operator)) {
                    result /= operand;
                }
            }
            display.setText(Double.toString(result));
        }
    }

}
3/7/23, 12:40 - Koustav Biswas DSATM: public class main {
	// Main method
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Calculator calculator = new Calculator();
    }
}

8/9/23, 12:52 - Koustav Biswas DSATM: package pkg1dt21cs072;

import java.util.Scanner;
public class Kruskals{
    static int parent[];
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        final int MAX = 20;
        int n;
        int cost[][]; 
        int a = 0, b = 0, u = 0, v = 0, ne = 1, min, mincost = 0;
        parent = new int[MAX]; 
        cost = new int[MAX][MAX];
        Scanner scan = new Scanner(System.in);
        System.out.println("Enter the no. of vertices");
        n = scan.nextInt();
        System.out.println("Enter the cost adjacency matrix");
        for (int i = 1; i <= n; i++) 
        for (int j = 1; j <= n; j++){
            cost[i][j] = scan.nextInt();
            if (cost[i][j] == 0)
                cost[i][j] = 999;
        }
        System.out.println("The edges of Minimum Cost Spanning Tree are");
        while (ne < n) {
            min= 999;
            for (int i =1; i <= n; i++) 
            for (int j = 1; j <= n; j++) 
                if (cost[i][j] < min) {                    
                    min = cost[i][j];
                    a = u = i; 
                    b = v = j;
                }
                u = find(u); 
                v = find(v);
                if (u != v) {                    
                    ne++;
                    System.out.println("edge " + a + "-->" + b + " =" + min);
                    mincost += min;
                    uni(a, v); 
                }
                cost[a][b] = cost[b][a] = 999; 
        }
        System.out.println("Minimum cost :" + mincost);
    }
    static int find(int i){        
        while (parent[i] != 0)
        i = parent[i];
        return i;
    }
    static void uni(int i, int j){        
        parent[j] = i;
    }
}
